    SELECT [w].[PrdFirstGroupID], [w].[FGName], [t].[WsproductSecondGroupId], [t].[Sgname], [w].[ParsaPooladMenusId]
    FROM [WSProductFirstGroup] AS [w]
    LEFT JOIN (
        SELECT [w0].[PrdSecondGroupID] AS [WsproductSecondGroupId], [w0].[SGName] AS [Sgname], [w0].[FirstGroupId]
        FROM [WSProductSecondGroup] AS [w0]
        WHERE [w0].[IsRemoved] IS NULL
    ) AS [t] ON [w].[PrdFirstGroupID] = [t].[FirstGroupId]
    WHERE [w].[IsRemoved] IS NULL
) AS [t0] ON [p].[ParsaPooladMenusId] = [t0].[ParsaPooladMenusId]
ORDER BY [p].[ParsaPooladMenusId], [t0].[PrdFirstGroupID], [t0].[WsproductSecondGroupId]" (0723d8ff)

FROM [ParsaPooladMenus] AS [p]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [w].[PrdFirstGroupID], [w].[FGName], [t].[WsproductSecondGroupId], [t].[Sgname], [w].[ParsaPooladMenusId]
    FROM [WSProductFirstGroup] AS [w]
    LEFT JOIN (
        SELECT [w0].[PrdSecondGroupID] AS [WsproductSecondGroupId], [w0].[SGName] AS [Sgname], [w0].[FirstGroupId]

    WHERE [w].[IsRemoved] IS NULL
) AS [t0] ON [p].[ParsaPooladMenusId] = [t0].[ParsaPooladMenusId]
